[y/n] [ACTION] yes [STATE] You shove off with all due haste. *** ***The return to civilization was a long one, but you both survived, and the long task of liquidating your assets finally began. Now, having dealt with numerous fences, suckers, and a few legitimate businessmen, you take inventory of your priceless treasures and how much they turned out to worth: The skull of an African gorilla, sold for 70 Spanish dollars to a credulous fellow already possessing the incomplete skeleton of an orangutan... A flawless crystal ball worth 60 dollars... A musky grey lump, later identified as a piece of rare ambergris, valued at 179 dollars... A cheap reproduction of a Ptolemaic statuette of the Egyptian god Thoth, melted down into lead ingots worth four dollars... An extraordinary Genevese music box worth 300 dollars... ...For a total of 613 Spanish dollars. The first mate's share of that came to 38 Spanish dollars and 2 reales. *** You and the Captain have both indulged in new coats, and the two of you draw many a glance as you stride down the street. "Really, I think we can take some time off," Verdeterre says. "We've got cash to live on for a good while, and something new will come up before we run out. Opportunities are constantly presenting themselves to me." He looks up at you approvingly. "Like you. I didn't have to hire you, but I did, and it seems to have worked out pretty okay." He smiles. "I doubt you could have done any better," he says, "and I really mean that." *** {Congratulations on your success.} *** Would you like to RESTART, RESTORE a saved game, QUIT, UNDO the last command, or read ABOUT this game?
